< review>
We decided to try this salon because they seemed to have good reviews. Sadly, I can't bring myself to agree with any of them. We called ahead to ask about pricing and schedule an appointment for two pedicures and a manicure. We were quoted a different price on the phone than we were actually charged. I was quoted $28 for each spa pedicure and $40 for acrylic nails. After seeing the product they used for acrylic, I changed my mind and decided to get shellac so I wouldn't damage my nails with poor quality acrylic. They charged me for the acrylic set, instead of the lower price shellac, and somehow, we ended up paying $50 for each pedi instead of the initial quoted price.
We learned a little too late that this place DOES NOT ACCEPT CREDIT CARDS so we were charged $8 total in ATM and bank fees to debit out cash.
Secondly, I had to wait so long to begin my pedicure that the water went cold in the whirlpool while they worked on my boyfriend's pedicure. When it was my turn for a pedicure, I was disappointed in the quality of the massage. It felt like she was scratching my skin rather than massaging the muscle.
I will say that it was nice that she used a salt scrub, but for $50 I would normally expect a mask. They used parafin wax instead, which is actually proven to dry your skin out in the long run.
After we left, we noticed there was still dirt on our toenails, and wax on our feet. I don't know how we ended up paying $140, but I will never go back to this spa again.</review>

<userid>101514302576478203342< /userid><Rate>5<//Rate>< text>
11-22-2015, Wow this place is GREAT, the owners are super nice and the food very tasty.  We had the Beef Kalbi and Daeji Bulugogi.  Both meat dishes were done to perfection.  If you like hot food be sure to tell them, they will put the real Korean heat to it, otherwise its going to be a nice medium hot for most novices. Prices compare to any other Korean BBQ in south San Jose and the friendly owners were definitely a bonus you don't find often. Can't wait to go back!< /text>
